All internal header storage uses this type.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/header_map_impl.cc`** and `header_map_impl.h` implement `HeaderMapImpl`, which stores all headers using `LowerCaseString` keys, enforcing lowercase at the storage layer.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.cc`** provides `ProperCaseHeaderKeyFormatter::format()`, which capitalizes HTTP/1.1 header names for outbound H1 responses (e.g., `content-type` → `Content-Type`). to HTTP/2 header normalization and translation logic in envoyproxy/envoy (v1.31.2) is spread across several layers:\\n\\n## 1. Header Case Normalization (Lowercase)\\n\\n**`envoy/http/header_map.h`** defines `LowerCaseString`, the core type that enforces lowercase normalization on all header names. Its constructor calls `lower()` which uses `absl::ascii_tolower` on every character. All internal header storage uses this type.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/header_map_impl.cc`** and `header_map_impl.h` implement `HeaderMapImpl`, which stores all headers using `LowerCaseString` keys, enforcing lowercase at the storage layer.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.cc`** provides `ProperCaseHeaderKeyFormatter::format()`, which capitalizes HTTP/1.1 header names for outbound H1 responses (e.g., `content-type` → `Content-Type`). This is the inverse: lowercased keys are re-cased for H1 wire format.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc`** (`ConnectionManagerUtility::mutateRequestHeaders`) calls `setScheme(absl::AsciiStrToLower(...))` to normalize the `:scheme` pseudo-header to lowercase.\\n\\n**`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc`** (`Http2HeaderValidator::validateGenericHeaderName`) enforces RFC 9113's requirement that HTTP/2 header names MUST be all lowercase (rejects uppercase characters in range 0x41–0x5a).\\n\\n## 2. Pseudo-Header Injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority)\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`** is the primary site where HTTP/1.1 request headers are parsed and pseudo-headers injected:\\n- `ServerConnectionImpl::handlePath()` (line ~1100): Sets `:path` from the request-target, `:scheme` (lowercased via `absl::AsciiStrToLower`) from absolute URLs, and `:authority` (via `setHost()`, which maps to `:authority` in Envoy's internal representation) from the Host header or absolute URL host.\\n- `ServerConnectionImpl::onHeadersCompleteBase()` (line ~1186): Calls `headers->setMethod(parser_->methodName())` to inject `:method`, calls `handlePath()` to inject `:path`/`:scheme`/`:authority`, then validates with `HeaderUtility::requestHeadersValid()`.\\n- `StreamEncoderImpl::encodeHeadersBase()` (line ~138): When encoding H2 headers back to H1 wire format, translates `:authority` → `host` (skips other pseudo-headers starting with `:`).\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.cc`** (`ServerConnectionImpl::onHeader`, line ~2306): Handles the special case where both `host` and `:authority` are present—discards `host` if `:authority` already set.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc`** (`ConnectionManagerUtility::mutateRequestHeaders`): Sets `:scheme` if missing, based on `X-Forwarded-Proto` or TLS status, and normalizes it to lowercase.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/header_utility.cc`** (`HeaderUtility::checkRequiredRequestHeaders`, `requestHeadersValid`): Validates the presence and validity of `:method`, `:path`, `:authority` pseudo-headers.\\n\\n**`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http1_header_validator.cc`** and **`http2_header_validator.cc`**: The UHV (Universal Header Validator) layer validates pseudo-headers (`:method`, `:authority`, `:scheme`, `:path`) for both H1 and H2 requests.\\n\\n## 3. Upgrade Header Handling (H1↔H2 Translation)\\n\\n**`source/common/http/utility.cc`** and **`utility.h`** contain the core upgrade transformation functions:\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2()`: Converts H1 `Upgrade: <protocol>` → H2 extended CONNECT (sets `:method: CONNECT`, `:protocol: <upgrade-value>`, removes `Upgrade` and `Connection` headers).\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeResponseFromH1toH2()`: Converts H1 `101 Switching Protocols` → H2 `200` response, removes `Upgrade`/`Connection`.\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeRequestFromH2toH1()`: Reverses the above—converts H2 extended CONNECT back to H1 `Upgrade` request.\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeResponseFromH2toH1()`: Converts H2 `200` extended CONNECT response back to H1 `101 Switching Protocols`.\\n- `Utility::isUpgrade()`, `Utility::isH2UpgradeRequest()`: Detection helpers.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.cc`**: Calls these transform functions in `ClientStreamImpl::encodeHeaders()` (H1→H2 direction when sending upstream) and `ServerStreamImpl::decodeHeaders()` (H2→H1 direction when receiving from upstream).\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`**: Handles upgrade detection (`handling_upgrade_`), blocks h2c upgrade requests, and controls chunk encoding bypass for upgraded connections.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc`** (`mutateRequestHeaders`): Preserves `Connection` and `Upgrade` headers for upgrade requests (skips hop-by-hop header removal).\\n\\n**`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc`**: The UHV layer performs the H1↔H2 upgrade transformation:\\n- `ServerHttp2HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders()`: Calls `transformUpgradeRequestFromH2toH1()` for incoming H2 extended CONNECT.\\n- `ServerHttp2HeaderValidator::transformResponseHeaders()`: Calls `transformUpgradeResponseFromH1toH2()` for outgoing responses.\\n- `ClientHttp2HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders()`: Calls `transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2()` for outgoing H1 upgrade requests going to H2 upstream.\\n- `ClientHttp2HeaderValidator::transformResponseHeaders()`: Calls `transformUpgradeResponseFromH2toH1()` for responses coming back from H2 upstream.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
